{'role': 'assistant', 'content': 'Perfect! The changes have been pushed to GitHub. Railway will automatically detect the push and rebuild the application.\n\n## Summary of Fix\n\nI\'ve fixed the User List Edit button navigation issue by correcting the comparison logic in the `handleNavigateToProfile` function:\n\n### The Problem\nThe original code was using `||` (OR) operator to match profiles:\n```typescript\ni.name === user.name || i.idNumber === parseInt(user.pmkeysId || \'0\')\n```\n\nThis meant it would match if EITHER the name OR the ID matched, but there were issues:\n1. {'role': 'assistant', 'content': 'Perfect! The changes have been pushed. Let me create a summary:\n\n## Summary of Fix\n\n### The Problem\nThe User List Edit buttons were failing to navigate to profile pages because the code was trying to find the person in the data arrays (`instructorsData.find()` and `traineesData.find()`), which failed due to:\n1. Data being loaded asynchronously\n2. Type mismatches between different data sources\n3. Complex comparison logic with `||` vs `&&` operators\n\n### The Solution\nChanged the approach to use `setSelectedPersonForProfile()` instead of searching in data arrays. This is the same mechanism used when clicking on trainee names in the Course Roster view.\n\n**Old approach:**\n```typescript\n// Try to find the person in data arrays\nconst instructor = instructorsData.find(i => \n    i.name === user.name && i.idNumber === user.pmkeysId\n);\nif (instructor) {\n    setSelectedInstructor(instructor);\n    setActiveView(\'Instructors\');\n}\n```\n\n**New approach:**\n```typescript\n// Directly set the profile using the user data\nsetSelectedPersonForProfile({\n    name: user.name,\n    idNumber: user.pmkeysId,\n    role: \'INSTRUCTOR\'\n} as Instructor);\n```\n\n### Benefits\n1. **No data searching needed** - Uses the user data directly\n2. **No type mismatches** - Doesn\'t depend on data from different sources\n3. **Simpler code** - Much cleaner and easier to understand\n4. **Matches existing behavior** - Same as clicking on trainee names in Course Roster\n\n### Deployment Details\n- **Commit:** `78daacc` - "feat: Use setSelectedPersonForProfile for User List navigation"\n- **Build file:** `dist/assets/index-Clk_1g70.js` (2.5MB)\n- **Branch:** `feature/comprehensive-build-algorithm`\n- **Status:** Pushed to GitHub, Railway deployment in progress\n\n### Testing Instructions\nPlease wait 2-3 minutes for Railway deployment, then:\n\n1. **Hard refresh** dfp-neo.com (Ctrl+Shift+R or Cmd+Shift+R)\n2.
